Yesterday and Today
Today, I will speak under the title 'Seokgeum (昔今), Yesterday and Today.' 
Yesterday and today have a chronological relationship. 
Our Unification Church does not have a long history. However, when does the origin of the Unification Church begin? It begins with the history of humanity, from the day God's providence began. This is how we view it. 
From the perspective of the Old Testament, the New Testament is the foundation of the future of the Old Testament, and from the center of the New Testament, the Unification Church is the foundation of the future of the New Testament. When we look at the New Testament, the Old Testament is seen as the foundation of the past. Today, when we center on the Unification Church, Christianity is the foundation of the past. When we consider the relationship of 'Seokgeum,' the relationship of 'Yesterday and Today,' it indicates that there is a chronological relationship. 
In your lifetime, there is the infancy stage, followed by the youth stage, adulthood, and old age. Similarly, we must understand that the course of providence connects such processes at any time. 
Therefore, if there were mistakes in the past, we must not repeat those mistakes today, and if there are mistakes today, we must innovate those mistakes starting tomorrow. We must go through new dimensions and new directions. Without doing so, we cannot reach the completion of the providence of restoration, the fulfillment of God's providence for salvation. 
When we look at this, let us think about those who followed God's will in the Old Testament and those who followed God's will in the New Testament. In the Old Testament, primitive forms of religion emerged, while in the New Testament, a contemporary religion emerged. In other words, the New Testament is a religious age that has continued to the modern civilization of the 20th century. What kind of religion is the Unification Church? The Unification Church must become a new dimension, a future-oriented religion, beyond primitive and contemporary religions. 
So, what is the ideal of our Unification Church? The ideal is the completion of the providence of salvation. What is the completion of the providence of salvation? It is to manifest the Kingdom of Heaven on earth. How can we manifest the Kingdom of Heaven on earth? Your faith life must be such that you live to establish the Kingdom of Heaven on earth from the day you believe until the day you die. This is the purpose. 
Therefore, whether each person establishes the Kingdom of Heaven on earth is a very serious issue. When Jesus was asked by his disciples, 'Where is the Kingdom of Heaven?' he said, 'The Kingdom is within your heart.' While it is said that the heart is the Kingdom, the practical Kingdom, the national Kingdom, and the global Kingdom cannot be found in the scriptures. It teaches that the future Kingdom will manifest, but it does not record that the Kingdom is established in the earthly world. The world is said to end with all judgment in the age of the Second Coming, but the scriptures do not teach that an ideal earthly Kingdom will manifest at the end of the world. 
When we look at this course of providence, the New Testament era and our era are of different dimensions. You must understand that the New Testament era and our era are of different dimensions. 
From the early days of the New Testament era, many sacrifices were made to develop Christianity. As you know, even if we focus on the 400 years of Roman persecution, countless people became sacrificial offerings, and through their sacrifices, Christianity expanded worldwide. 
 The Kingdom is a place centered on God.
So, what about the era of the Unification Church? Until today, the Unification Church has been going for 37 years since its inception right after liberation. This is seen as entering a new dimension with 40 years as a boundary. Therefore, this period corresponds to what the scriptures refer to as the wilderness period. Thus, it is believed that we are entering a new dimension with the 40-year mark as a turning point. 
So, what should we do when we reach the 40-year stage? We must transcend the national level and move toward the world. The path to that world should not be one of persecution, but one of welcome, and if so, the path of our Unification Church will enter a period of leap. 
Then, has the life of the Unification Church, as proclaimed by the Unification Church, been a life of the Kingdom of Heaven on earth? This is the question. When we consider our Unification Church, which is in the position of trying to realize the Kingdom of Heaven on earth, it is a serious question whether the Unification Church itself has the past to construct the Kingdom of Heaven on earth. 
What is the Kingdom? The Kingdom is where God is present; it is a place where, with God's presence, the angelic world and the good spiritual realm can harmonize and live together, a place where there are no opposing phenomena of Satan. 
Until now, we have thought about constructing such a Kingdom, but the truth is that we ourselves have not entered the Kingdom. We are in the position of heading toward the Kingdom. 
So, can we say that each individual heading toward the Kingdom has the qualification to enter the Kingdom? This is the issue. Are we qualified? This is the problem. Have we become citizens of the Kingdom? Not only citizens but have we become direct children of God? This is a significant issue. Direct children of God have the privilege to possess all of God's possessions. Wherever God is, wherever God goes, we can go. There are no borders where God wants to go. It is a place where everyone can create an environment of welcome. In this sense, if we have become citizens of Heaven who can enter the Kingdom, we can enter anywhere by ourselves. In that sense, what is the problem? This is serious. 
If Satan exists, Satan will not just sit idle until the Kingdom is established on earth. Until the Kingdom is established, Satan will oppose it. This indicates that the moment of final decision between Satan and myself is approaching. Therefore, in order for you to become a people of the Kingdom, you must not leave any conditions for Satan's accusations. 
Then, what are the conditions for Satan's accusations? Until entering the Kingdom, one can mix and mingle, but once one crosses over, one cannot enter with conditions for Satan's accusations. It must be settled. A thorough settlement must be made. If there is a family, the husband must make that decision centered on the family, and if there is a wife, she must make that decision herself, and if there are children, they must all make that decision. A settlement must be made. There must be such a settlement at the forefront of heading toward the Kingdom on earth. 
Then, the question is, what are the conditions for Satan's accusations? This includes content related to your fallen nature, but it must necessarily center on oneself…. 
What is the Kingdom centered on? It is not centered on oneself. It is centered on God. It starts from God, not from me. Because the Kingdom starts from God, I must become a person from God. 
A person on God's side, a person representing God must have a mindset like God's. One must think like God and act in a way that can represent God's activities. 
Everyone has desires. There are desires for possessions, desires for honor, and desires for justice, but one must not involve oneself in these desires. One must exercise ownership centered on God. My whole life must be for the purpose of glorifying God's name, and even in emotional matters, when it comes to love, that love should not be for myself but should be connected to the whole and for God. 
 Humans must determine ownership for God.
So, what is the biggest problem in entering the Kingdom? The enemy called 'I' is lurking. I am the enemy. Until now, everything you have prayed for and worked hard for in your faith life has been to overcome yourself. It is to win over the conditions for Satan's accusations. As long as 'I' exists, this is completely…. 
Next, one must become a person who denies oneself, a person who denies oneself in the name of God. One must completely deny oneself. It must be a complete denial. Only then can all the strings that Satan has been following be completely cut off. You see, it is like a thread that is stretched across the world. It must be cut off with something as sharp as a razor. 
Satan finds a path for accusations through the conditions of our desires. It comes seeking through the conditions of desire. So, the problem is, 'This is all mine!' How do we overcome this? We must say, 'This is from the Father, from Heaven. It belongs to Heaven.' Before it becomes mine, it must first be God's. 
Why is that? Because when humans fell, God could not stand in the position of ownership. Although all things were created as God's, due to the fall of humanity, who became the owner? Love is love, but it is false love. Centered on love, the universe is supposed to be under God's dominion, but due to the fall, it has entered under Satan's dominion, and thus all things have entered into the realm of false love centered on false love, all belonging to Satan. All things are like that, and humanity is like that. The spiritual realm has also entered under Satan's dominion. Although all things were for humanity and humanity was for God, all beings in the world of existence have not received the determination of God's ownership. You must understand that. They have lost the right to determine ownership. 
God made Adam and Eve as His sons and daughters, but what was the most essential requirement for making them His sons and daughters? It was based on the proposition of love centered on God…. Because they could not reach the position of being called His sons and daughters centered on love, they lost everything as humans. Because God lost ownership, we humans are in a position where we must determine ownership for God. When we say we have made a determination of ownership, the conditions for Satan's accusations must be completely denied. 
You see, right? There must be grandmothers here. 'The husband I lived with in the past did not know the Unification Church or God, but he has passed away. Now that I think about it, I miss that husband.' If you think, 'Ah, that husband! I will meet him in the spiritual world!' how would that be? That cannot be accepted. It cannot be permitted. 
When you see yourself as a beloved daughter of God, you must completely settle the conditions for Satan's accusations. To transcend the issue of love in a static sense, you must…. That affection for your old husband is not on God's side. It is not love centered on God. That was merely a man who appeared through all the relationships in the world of Satan, not a husband who stood in a position settled with Satan. 
Today, as you, the grandmothers of the Unification Church, are about to enter the Kingdom, have you settled everything? If you are in a static position and long for your old husband, through that condition of longing for your old husband, Satan can use that as a bridge to come over. 
Then, regarding children…. 'Oh, I must enter the Kingdom….' Even if you are destined to enter the Kingdom, if you think, 'Oh, my eldest son, my eldest daughter! What about my grandchildren?' what will happen? Think about it. What will happen? Unless they have no relation to the will, Heaven will not permit it. It cannot be permitted to enter the Kingdom. If it were allowed, through your sons and daughters, Satan would always be able to come and go. It would always be able to come and go in your emotional world. If you have such a self that can come and go, even if you enter the Kingdom, Satan can always pull you back. If you long for this more than for God, you must turn back. 
So, in the static realm, to whom must you become a complete and absolute possession? To God. The reason we emphasize absolute faith is because of this. God is the absolute one. Regarding the husband, the wife must also give that ownership to God…. You must love and live under God's protection. It is not yours. This is not mine; it is God's, it is the universe's. As a representative woman, it is absolutely necessary to have the concept and thought of meeting and living to spread and illuminate God's love in the universe. At some point, a settlement must be made. At some point, a settlement must be made. 
When viewed from the emotional realm, if there are two people, and you love both equally as a parent, if anyone thinks even slightly differently, there will be jealousy, and there will be a desire to center on oneself and show oneself. So, what do you do about that? In the fallen world, that cannot be permitted. 
Today, young people who have entered the Unification Church say, 'Ah, since I have entered the Unification Church, I must become a great person.' Are there people like that? 
Why is this lady smiling with her mouth open? (Laughter) What kind of deacon is she? What does she want me to do by smiling with my mouth open? Does she want me to give her some candy? (Laughter) Why is she sitting in front? She should sit in the back. If you sit in the front, the responsibility is great. When Satan looks, it will be the first to be checked. If they start checking from the front row, you will be the first to be checked. If you are in the back, they might not find you…. What is this?
"I was wrong" (laughter) If I was wrong, everything is connected. That's a nice way to put it. What can we do when someone says, "I was wrong"? (laughter) We're talking about something very serious here... Ah, when you come out after marrying your spouse... Everyone, didn't you come out after marrying your spouse to go to heaven? Do you think about your spouse these days? Do you think about your spouse? "We have to save them." What does that mean? When you're entering heaven, wouldn't you just take one step into heaven? Do you really have to come out and say you want to save them even after entering the heavenly gate? I'm talking about something serious, and your expression while you were speaking was quite impressive. (laughter)

The past and present must be certain for the future to be certain. Here in the Unification Church, among the older people, what should we call them? The so-called people of the old era of the Unification Church, if we look at them centered around the Unification Church, they are like people from the Old Testament era, right? They cannot be people of the New Testament era. If Grandpa Noah or Grandpa Abraham were to come and say to Jesus, "Hey, Jesus! Didn't you know I'm your grandfather?" would that make sense? It wouldn't make sense. Jesus is in the position of the parents. No matter how many thousands of years ago they were grandfathers, they cannot act recklessly in front of Jesus, who stands in the position of a parent. Today, the grandfathers and grandmothers of the Unification Church say, "We came in first..." but that is a story from the Old Testament era, and the story of entering heaven in the New Testament era is different. Can all the old people from the past enter heaven? I don't think so.

So now I'm talking about the past and present. As today goes on, the time for us to enter heaven through our faithfulness will come quickly on this earth. 

So what would happen if all of South Korea became Unification Church? Would it just be so-so, or would it seem like it would be a time of reckoning? It should be a time of reckoning. Once you enter the Unification Church, you must record all of history yourself. You must record how you lived, what you did, and what path you took. There can be no objections to that. "Oh, there were some things I opposed in the past, but now that I'm in this position, let's leave that out!" That won't work. It must be revealed. You must record all the conditions of your life. By clearly recording the past and present, it serves as a solid foundation for a certain future... The past must be certain, and the present must be certain to form a solid foundation for a certain future. Isn't that so? The foundation here should not be like a rubber band that can stretch when Satan pulls it. It must be a foundation that is completely settled.

So then, what about the teacher himself? When the time comes for the world to enter the heavenly kingdom, what will happen to the spirits of the Unification Church that I raised and brought along with great care? Do you know what a spirit is? A spirit is a ghost cousin. (laughter) What will happen to the 36 families? They must be completely settled, completely. Satan accuses, and everything that can come in according to Satan must be organized and completely severed. It must be completely severed. Isn't it sad? Isn't it regrettable? Isn't it? It is regrettable.

All possessions related to me must first belong to God. Until now, I've followed the teacher all my life, but when it comes time to enter the heavenly gate, everything gets cut off, and the door slams shut behind me. (laughter) Once it's shut, it cannot be opened again. It cannot be opened. If Satan opens it, everyone runs away. Only I can open and close it, come in and out.

There must be a determination that Satan cannot open it and that no one else can come in and out. This applies not only to the members of the Unification Church but also to their parents and relatives. They will build a bridge through their parents to come in... So when the Bible says, "Your family members are your enemies," it is seen in that context.

The attitude towards the will must become more serious as the time approaches, rather than becoming lax. All possessions or desires related to me, such as honor, must first belong to God. They must belong to God first. We must inherit the essence of all those desires from God, but due to the fall, God has departed.

Therefore, to put it simply, Jesus said, "Those who want to die will live, and those who want to live will die." What does that mean? There is a realm that cannot be reached, a realm that cannot be reached. As this Unification Church becomes more famous, many people want to meet the teacher. So, I try not to meet them as much as possible, and so-called elders here... They will do anything to meet the teacher... If I meet them, they will feel proud. That's a problem too.

This time, I didn't even think about it, but there was a conference for the Principle Research Association, then the Victory Committee Conference, and then some interdenominational... They stood behind me to enter the heavenly gate, saying, "Ah, interdenominational advisory committee?" "Yes, that's right," "Retreat!" Should it be like that? (laughter) "Oh, okay, okay," and then turn around... It cannot be like that. There must be a time for that.

Then everything related to me will say, "Teacher, please wait a moment! I have to take you!" There will be all sorts of noises. "Why are you leaving me like this? You can't do that!" If I hear that, should I say, "Okay, let's do that!"? What do you think? Should I step forward or step back? Should I step forward or step back? "I must step forward." God is a God of justice. But the things of the Unification Church are saying, "No, no, no! Back, back..." (laughter) Then what should I do? Answer me. What should I do? Should I step back or step forward? 

What about those women? Are the men and women all mixed together? Is there a woman with a beard over there? Oh, it's a man! (laughter) They don't even realize they're talking about themselves and are laughing out loud... They might be dull about that, so they'll probably sit there. So, should I step back or step forward? "I must step forward." That's the right answer. (laughter) Anyway, when you go to the spiritual world, such things will happen. Whether you like it or not, such things exist between you and the teacher. Isn't that so? If you try to do this or that and get caught up in some conditions, the teacher cannot cross the boundary to go, and there are many ways that cannot be crossed.

When God judged Sodom and Gomorrah, He told Lot's wife not to look back, but she looked back and was turned into a pillar of salt, right? Didn't that happen? Such a time exists for everyone.

The world and heaven are different. The world is under the dominion of Satan. While living in the world, everything—possessions, desires, everything—no matter how wonderful it is, cannot be severed from Satan completely. It must be cut off.

Therefore, one must not become a heartless person. You must become a cruel person! What kind of person must you become? "You must not become a heartless person..." No, you must become a cruel person! What happens if the teacher is so heartless? Will they say, "Hallelujah, Amen!"? 

When I was in America, there were people who had been in the church for a long time, and when they came to America, they would say, "I'm here! Take me on a world tour!" It's all like that. "I'm here!" Who recognizes me? When I ask, "Why did you come?" they say, "What do you mean why? I came to go on a world tour." Is that something that will be accepted in heaven or not? Where is your answer? We must think about the principled issue. That won't work.

They kick me out and say, "I'm a busy person." If they cooperate with busy work, I would welcome it, but they must not interfere with busy work. That's how it is. Is that a correct statement or not? "That's a correct statement." Those older people, is that a correct statement or not? "That's correct." Right. Is there someone saying, "Hey, take me to America and show me around?" "No." (laughter) What? "No." What do you mean no? That's regrettable.

One must be willing to die for God for Satan to leave. A person doing great things must be believed by their wife. When a husband begins the path of a patriot for the country, the wife must not say, "Oh, where are you going? What about the children, and what about me...?" That is a decisive moment in whether one becomes a patriot or not. At that time, if you have a knife, you must cut the wife's hand, and if you cannot have courage after that, you cannot walk the path of a patriot. Even if the parents try to stop you, you must cut off and go.

If this is the case for loving the country and walking the path of patriotism... Only those who do not just love their country can enter heaven. Didn't even the saint Jesus himself not enter heaven? Isn't that so, even for the Son of God? Therefore, other saints, whether it be Buddha or Confucius, no matter what they did, they also could not enter heaven. To enter heaven, one must prepare in this world.

What is the issue? Since Jesus could not enter heaven, to enter heaven, one must decide all the procedures and emotional content that can allow them to enter heaven before they go. If you do not do that and when you are about to enter heaven, say, "Can I enter without knowing me?" at that moment, it cannot happen. Such a serious issue is placed before the path you are taking.

Moreover, various cords from the world of Satan behind us entangle my limbs. They entangle me like electric wires and pull me. Just a little bit of a snag pulls me. It drags me around. If that happens, what is the biggest problem in entering heaven? The nation is the enemy. The emergence of hell and the world of Satan arose from self-awareness. The archangel thought, "What will happen to me?" and centered around me. 

What is a traitor? A person who thinks beyond the nation and the sovereign centered around themselves is called a traitor. The peak that rides on me is all connected to the path of the traitor. It is connected to the path of hell. It is connected to the path of human destruction. Isn't that so? This nation, this foundation centered around me, is connected to death. I think there are many people in my clan who were slaughtered by the communist Kim Il-sung because of me. My family may have been exterminated because of me. I have that background, but I don't even want to think about it, nor do I pray.

Thinking about the sacrificed cow, "Ah! That cow was good; I wish I had that cow again," that thought itself becomes irreverent. Do you understand what I mean? My clan must have gone through such things before God. If they were sacrificed, God took them as a sacrificial offering. To fulfill this cosmic mission I must undertake, those closest to me must have been sacrificed, so thinking that I miss and regret those who were sacrificed does not align with the will. I am cruel. Isn't that so? Do you understand what I mean?

If you regret the money or anything you have collected with sincerity after placing it on the altar and offering it, you will be punished. It would be better not to offer it at all. You all know the story of Ananias and Sapphira in the Bible, right? They sold their property and thought they could do whatever they wanted, hiding half and bringing only half, and ended up being punished. The term "all" means that whether you offer it or not, it is all considered as an offering. If you hide it, you will receive a penalty for that, and the game of punishment occurs. Do you understand? Holding onto the fact of being offered and thinking about your own possessive nature is not allowed. Do you understand?

If there are such stories, everything must be settled before the time comes. Before the time comes, before crossing the hill, everything must be settled. I must think about the responsibility I cannot bear and settle everything. I must find myself that can prepare for that day. 

In this regard, if the Unification Church is to present the task of being the earthly kingdom of heaven, there will come a time when we must cross the borders of the world of Satan. Do you understand what I mean? If there is a 38th parallel, people from North Hamgyong or South Hamgyong or North Pyongan or South Pyongan cannot come to the South without crossing the 38th parallel. If they cannot cross that, they will have to go back and be oppressed in that world, and similarly, if you cannot cross the 38th parallel in front of you, you must understand that this nation will perish. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes."
Repent of the ownership concept centered on this.  
What is the difference between families blessed by the Unification Church and families in the world?  
What is different about families blessed by the Unification Church? In that sense, they are different. Blessed families can be recognized as having heaven's approved love centered on their wives and children. Blessed individuals have the privilege to think and reason for themselves. Even if they cannot be in the same place, just thinking about it allows them to escape the conditions of Satan's accusations. Do you understand?  
What is different about blessed families? Blessed families can wait in the buffer zone of the boundary. What does that mean? When I enter the heavenly gate, thinking of my sons and daughters, my wife does not become a condition for Satan's accusations and is recognized. That is the difference. Do you understand? Therefore, loving your wife and going to that country is recognized. Those who are married in the world of Satan are not recognized. That is the difference. Do you understand?  
The good thing about blessed people is this. Even if you have a husband or wife, when I cross the border, I can think of and pray for that wife and husband. When you think that way, isn't it wonderful? "Yes."  
Also, why are the children of Unification Church members good? When entering the heavenly gate, even if they call out to their mother, father, or siblings, Satan cannot accuse them. That is the difference. Do you understand? "Yes." That is different. They did not know the tremendous fact that such privileges were granted. "What good is being blessed? If I had married according to my heart, I could have found a better husband or wife..." They did not know that. The husband I obtained freely always has the strings of Satan attached to him. Do you understand? The strings of Satan are attached.  
When blessed families try to follow the teacher 100 percent in that sense, it is okay to search and wait. It is possible within the limits that can be permitted, but otherwise, no matter how hard you try, it will not work. Has everyone been blessed? Raise your hand if you are blessed. Put your hands down. This is to clearly distinguish between blessed families and unblessed families. At some point, when there is a command from above, there will be a time when you must leave without notifying relatives or others. You need to understand that. Do you understand? "Yes." There is a time similar to when a wife told her husband, "Honey, if you follow me, you can live," and they left. You need to know that.  
Among the Israelites, it is okay to notify each other, but notifying the Egyptians is recognized by God as a sin.  
Now, after our Unification Church teacher has said everything, he turns away. Once he turns away, he does not turn back again. That is the same with heaven; once it turns away, it does not return.  
Your past and today are different. Yesterday and today are different. Yesterday and today are different. When entering heaven, it is not the church that enters first. It starts with one person.  
In the Unification Church, it will be the representative teacher who enters first, right? "Yes." Then, will you take your mother with you, or will you follow your mother? "I will follow her." (Laughter) Oh, don’t laugh. This is a serious matter. Will you take her with you, or will you follow her? "I will take her with me." (Laughter) This is a serious matter. Should I follow my mother in, or should I take her with me? "I must take her with me." What about the mother? What should the mother do? "She must take the father with her."  
No matter how you take her, it is still taking her. But which one starts first? You must know that you should take God with you and then take your mother. Do you understand? You must understand this clearly. You must take God with you… The mother must follow. Isn’t that right? How can you take your mother with you when you are taking God? (Laughter) Is there such a law? The mother must go without hesitation. You should like it and say, "Thank you, Teacher, for taking me instead"—at that time, the teacher is more important than your husband (laughs)—and you must follow him in. You must understand this clearly. No matter how much you love your wife, when you take God with you… When you have seated God, then you may be able to take your mother. Before that, you must follow. You must follow.  
You must deny everything to be reborn from God.  
That is why men must understand this. There are many women who want to dominate men. From what I hear, in Taiwan… Who is the Zhang? "It’s Park." Is the husband Zhang? "Yes." That person can dominate her husband easily, looking at her forehead or nose. (Laughter) But at that time, the husband must follow. "Ah! You, stand behind me!" cannot be done. You cannot enter like that. When entering according to principle, the man must be the subject and stand in front; that is the original principle. The original principle is the constant of heaven, and the teachings of humanity are the principles of human nature, right? Do you know Park Chi-seong? Is the husband too easygoing? Is the husband not here? "He is sitting in the back." Park Chi-seong’s husband! (Laughter) Don’t let yourself be dominated by women. (Laughter) The teacher has already organized these issues.  
When the entire Republic of Korea says, "Let’s all believe in the Unification Church!" and the Unification Church becomes the national religion, what will happen to the teacher? He will become someone who can teach even the president, right? "Yes." When that happens, can you freely enter where the teacher is? (Laughter) Think about it. Can you just go freely? "No, you cannot." You cannot, right? Even if the teacher's parents come and say, "Ah! I am so-and-so's mother and father," they will still say, "Is that so? Please wait a moment." "What do you mean wait?" It won’t work. "Why must I wait?" "There is a procedure." (Laughter) Isn’t that so? Even if it is your mother, you must check and verify her name and photo, and the watchman must stamp the okay before you can enter; you cannot enter before that. Is that right or not? "That’s right." That is correct. You must go through that procedure.  
Everyone needs such procedures when entering heaven. No matter how well you know the teacher, no matter how close you are, even if you have spent the night together, it will not work. The business through fish powder

Even frozen fish, after eight months, needs water to be supplied again, and even if the ice has frozen, due to climate differences, air gets in. When air gets in, moisture from the fish escapes through the ice. Do you understand? (laughs) So, you have to sprinkle water all over and refreeze it to put it back in. That’s not feasible. Our Oath
Everyone, if you look at the Chinese characters, the meaning is profound. The character for oath (盟誓) has the character for alliance (盟), which means the sun and the moon, and the character for plate (皿; meaning vessel) as well. The character for oath (誓) has the meaning of continuing and also of cutting. If you continue to speak as intended, it means declaring by cutting. Although it is a Chinese-style notation, there are many interpretations. There are historical records saying that it was created by Koreans.

An oath is a promise made before God regarding the future.
In ancient times, the Dongyi tribe of Korea was a cultural nation centered around the Beijing coast, and even Confucius admired Koreans greatly. If you look at the history of China during the Shang Dynasty, it is said that people like Qin Shi Huang were originally Korean, and there are historical materials to support that. So, what the teacher is currently planning is to organize an association to clarify this with Chinese scholars, Japanese scholars, and Korean scholars. That is the task from now on.

The meaning of an oath is, first, to promise before God, and second, to promise regarding the future. Now, we have an oath document. The first oath in that document states that God created the universe, but because He lost the created world, it speaks of the loss of the universe, the loss of sons and daughters, the authority of God, and the ideal. the influence of Christianity was significant in establishing social order and cultural development. Buddhism in India also played a crucial role in promoting peace and ethical conduct among the people. 

In summary, the establishment of an absolute value system is essential for resolving the current global chaos. This can only be achieved through a religious framework that acknowledges and reveres God. The teachings and principles derived from such religions provide the foundation for a unified understanding of truth and values, which are necessary for the survival and flourishing of humanity. 

Thus, it is imperative that we recognize the importance of returning to these absolute values and truths in order to create a harmonious world free from conflict and division. Only through this collective effort can we hope to overcome the challenges we face and build a future that reflects the ideals of love, peace, and unity.
The Christian culture of the West was like this, and the Buddhist culture of ancient India during the Ashoka period was similarly characterized. Additionally, the Islamic civilization in the Middle East (Saracen civilization) is one of the prominent examples of this.

The Collapse of Religious Values and Its Causes
Unfortunately, as of today, religion, regardless of its type, has lost its ability to resolve chaos and guide the human spirit. Nowadays, religion is gradually losing its vitality, and faith is becoming increasingly formalized. Humanity is drifting away from religion, and the original attitude of faith that should burn like a blazing fire is fading away, except for a few examples. This is indeed a serious situation. When religion, which should lead the spirit of humanity, completely loses its function, the world will turn into a lawless land, and humanity will plunge into a sea of violence, chaos, and slaughter. In fact, such phenomena have already begun to occur today and are being accelerated by the strategies of communism. This can be succinctly described as the phenomenon of the collapse of religious values.

So, what are the causes of this collapse? Firstly, it is due to the development of science and technology and economic growth, which have led the human spirit toward materialism. Secondly, various forms of atheism and materialism, led by communism, are rapidly and widely spreading. Thirdly, under the name of political division, the exclusion of religion from educational policies results in the indoctrination of atheistic ideas from a young age. Fourthly, communists are intentionally using strategies to destroy the remaining values for their red infiltration efforts. Fifthly, there is a lack of a solid ontology that should theoretically defend religious values.

Among these, the most important is the lack of ontology. Ontology refers to the theory concerning the absolute being. Each religion has an absolute being that serves as the basis for its doctrines. The absolute being of Judaism is Yahweh, the absolute being of Christianity is God, and the absolute being of Islam is Allah. Although Confucianism and Buddhism do not explicitly state an absolute being, the fundamental virtue of Confucianism, 'ren (仁)', is connected to the mandate of heaven, so 'heaven (天)' can be seen as the absolute being of Confucianism, while Buddhism states that all phenomena are constantly changing and that truth can be found in the 'tathata (真如)' behind all phenomena, which can be considered the absolute being of Buddhism.

However, the explanations concerning these absolute beings are extremely ambiguous. The attributes of the absolute being, why creation occurred, what the motivation for creation was, how creation was accomplished, and whether God (the absolute being) actually exists are not clearly explained in any religion. Therefore, since the basis for the virtues of each religion is uncertain, the persuasive power of religion is weakening today.

Disputes Over Ontology and Religion
For the teachings of all religions, namely the virtues or practical principles, to be well observed, the attributes of the absolute being, the purpose of creation, and the existence of that absolute being must be sufficiently clarified. Until the medieval period or before the modern era, human thought was not very analytical or logical, so when it was said, 'Love your neighbor as yourself,' or 'Be loyal to the king and filial to your parents,' people unconditionally accepted and obeyed those teachings. However, in today's developed scientific age, human thought has become highly analytical and logical, so no matter how much a religious leader teaches 'to do this or that,' people will question 'why should it be so?' Therefore, if this counter-question is not answered, the teaching loses its persuasive power.

There are various counter-questions to religious teachings. 'Does God really exist?' 'God is described as omniscient, omnipotent, omnipresent, the ultimate good, the ultimate beauty, love, the lord of judgment, and the father of humanity, but how can we know that is true?' 'If God could have remained idle, why did He create the universe?' 'What is the purpose of God's creation?' 'There must have been a method for creation; what was that method?' 'Why is there a phenomenon of survival of the fittest in a world created by the absolute good God?' 'It is said that humanity fell into sin, but why did the perfect God create humans who would fall?' These are some of the questions.

Unless reasonable answers are provided to these counter-questions, today's intellectuals are reluctant to accept religion (for example, Christianity). As a result, the virtues of love in Christianity, the norms of family ethics in Confucianism, the practical principles of practice in Buddhism, and the principles in the Quran of Islam are discarded, and sometimes intellectuals even engage in anti-religious actions.

Historically, the emergence of materialism and atheism in the soil of Christianity's world, Europe (the West and the East), after the modern era, which now dominates the world, fundamentally stems from the ambiguity of this ontology. The most notable examples are Marx, Lenin, Stalin, and Nietzsche, who were born into Christian families yet became atheists and anti-Christian figures.

Moreover, it is lamentable that the religion, which should mediate human conflicts and lead the human spirit, is sometimes causing disputes today, further diminishing the prestige and authority of religion. Judaism and Islam are fighting, old and new churches are in conflict, Christianity and Buddhism are at odds, and even factions within the same religion are fighting. The fundamental cause of these religious disputes also lies in the ambiguity of ontology. There can only be one absolute being, and there cannot be two or three; however, the leaders of each religion believe that only their absolute being is the true God, and that all other gods are not true gods, resulting in the conclusion that each religion has its own absolute being, which establishes the contradiction that there are multiple absolute beings. Therefore, ultimately, this can be rephrased to conclude that the gods of all religions are merely relative gods, and the absolute value system that was supposed to be established through each religion, namely the theory concerning God's love and truth, remains relative. In other words, it concludes that until now, religion has been unable to establish an absolute value system capable of resolving chaos. This is an inevitable result of all religions failing to provide a precise explanation regarding the absolute being.

The Emergence of New Religions and the Establishment of Absolute Values
In this situation, to establish an absolute value system, it is logically necessary for a new religion with an ontology that provides an accurate and correct explanation of the unique, absolute God to emerge.

Previously, various religions were considered to be established by God, and it was assumed that absolute values were realized through these religions; however, seeing the religious disputes today, it can be confirmed that the gods of each religion cannot be the absolute God and that an absolute value system cannot be established through the existing religions. Therefore, the conclusion is reached that a new religion must emerge to establish an absolute value system.

The new ontology for the new religion must clarify that all previous absolute beings are not separate gods but rather the same one God. At the same time, it should be able to show that the understanding of some attributes of that God is what each religion's view of God is, and that all religions are brotherly religions established by one God. Furthermore, this ontology must clarify the attributes of God along with the motivation for creation, the purpose of creation, and the laws governing that purpose and law, showing that these govern the movement of all things in the universe and that the norms humans must adhere to ultimately align with the laws of the universe, that is, the heavenly way.

Just as the laws of creation of the sun, moon, and stars establish a vertical order in the universe, there should also be established a vertical order consisting of grandparents, parents, and children in families, as well as a horizontal order consisting of siblings, simultaneously establishing corresponding value systems, that is, norms. Moreover, this ontology should not contradict natural scientific knowledge, should be acceptable by the judgments of human conscience, and should further prove that throughout history, the proposition 'those who go against heaven perish, and those who follow heaven endure' has been applicable. The value system established by this ontology will be the true meaning of absolute values, and through understanding and practicing these absolute values (absolute truth, absolute goodness, absolute beauty), a spiritual reform of humanity will be achieved, and the chaos of the world will gradually disappear.

Unity of New Ontology and Religion
When everything concerning God is explained by the new ontology and it is revealed that the gods of all religions are ultimately the same one absolute God, a substantial unity of religion will be achieved while each religion maintains its own label, and they will work together to realize the ideal of God's creation, the kingdom of heaven on earth.

Moreover, the deficiencies and unresolved issues in the doctrines of all religions will be supplemented by the new ontology, leading to the realization of substantial doctrinal unity. Thus, all religions will finally achieve the purpose for which God established those religions.

In conclusion, the Unification Church has emerged as a new religion to solve the issues concerning the absolute value system that can resolve today's global chaos, and its content is broad and theoretical, even claiming to brainwash intellectuals through its famous Unification principles and Unification thought.

I hope that the continuous efforts and research of all of you attending this conference will deepen your understanding of absolute values, and I pray that God's grace will be with you. Thank you.

Now, if you see, there is no place where an Eastern person can laugh like this with Western people, 'ha ha ha, ho ho ho.' Also, white people say they will die if they don’t sit in a chair, but here, sitting on the floor, just saying 'whatever will be, will be' is there any other place like this? In the Western world, everyone sits in pointed churches and says, '15 minutes of worship, no more than 40 minutes,' and here, it’s okay to do it for 4 hours, 10 hours, 'ha ha ha.' (laughter) So this must be a spectacle for God. 
Now, would God only be interested? Just getting scolded and saying he will earn money and not spend it, but use it all for the world. Are these people crazy or really smart? Think about it. If God exists, He cannot be on our side. 
Do you want to listen to your husband, your wife, your teacher, or God? "God’s words." That’s right. Now, if Reverend Moon says, 'You two have passed 30 years, so live together,' but God says, 'No!' what will happen? If Reverend Moon says, 'You are over 30, so you should have children. The principle of creation says you should hurry and have them,' and God says, 'No!' what will happen? Should that be canceled or not? "It should be canceled." 
Also, if you and your husband decide to finish early today and go to the theater, but the teacher says 'no,' what should you do? "You shouldn’t go." In that case, you shouldn’t go. Similarly, no matter how much Reverend Moon allows, when God says 'no,' you must say, 'Yes, I understand.' That’s right. Such things will happen. 
Now, do you like living in debt or not living in debt? "Not living in debt…" Now, which is better, dating while in debt and going to the theater, or separating with your bags and saying goodbye? Which is better, the first or the second? "The second is better." Is the second better, or is the first better? "The second." The first! "The second." The first! "The second." The first is better! "The second." I am the teacher, so you must follow my words. (laughter) The first! "The second is better." Truth has power, even more than the teacher. (laughter) Now, let’s stop here. This is a big deal. Let’s finish today and continue next time. How about that? "No." There’s not just part one, but part two, part three, part four as well. (laughter) 
All our institutions are made for the other
So, when we look at this, it is absolute that the body and mind must unite centered on the heart. This is a heavenly principle. It is a public law. You must understand that. The world of existence and the world of consciousness, the physical world and the spiritual world, the earthly nation and the heavenly nation all harmonize, so in front of the truth, there is harmony. 
When you stand in front of the mirror in the morning and look at yourself, you can immediately tell whether you are thinking physically or mentally by looking into your eyes. Your eyes symbolize God, so you must know that they are foretelling what you are thinking. When you look into your eyes and say, "Hey, don’t you like this conscious world?" it will say, "Yes, yes." Then when you say, "Now we need to go fundraising," how should your eyes respond? Should they cry? They should smile. 
Next is the nose! The nose symbolizes Adam and Eve. It is the center of the universe. The nose grows the latest. The nose is the last to develop among the human body parts. So it is the center of the universe. It is the bridge connecting heaven and earth. It is the bridge connecting the physical and spiritual. 
Now, is it good if one nostril is blocked? "We need to get married." When you get married, it becomes two nostrils. "Nose, you must receive the heavenly command from above and convey it correctly to the earth, you little brat! That’s an order." It must respond, "Yes, yes, yes." The best answer is "Yes!" In the morning, before washing your face, you must warn yourself, "You must always speak one word; you must not speak two." "You little ear, you must listen to the right things." Then the hands and feet…. There are nine parts. "You little hand, you can’t just grab anyone!" This means your heart says, "Oh, don’t grab the hand of another man’s wife." How is that? Nine parts. If you count, it’s one, two, three, four, five, six, seven, eight, nine, ten, eleven, twelve. Two eyes, two nostrils, two ears, one mouth, two arms, two legs, where did one go? It must be twelve, twelve. (pointing to what he wrote) Ten, eleven. Then what is it? It’s twelve, but where did one go? Where did one go? "The torso." No. That is your reproductive organ. 
You must control this. "You little eye!" and you must not let your eyes wander freely.
You have to do it. The same goes for smell. The five senses are mobilized at once; they are relative, relative. You need to understand that. When a woman appears to a man, everything goes there: the eyes go there, the nose goes there, the mouth goes there, the ears go there, the hands go there, and the feet all go there. 

If you ask the eyes, "What do you want to see?" what do you think they would say? If you ask a woman's eyes, there is no eye that would answer, "I want to see a woman." They would say, "I want to see the rough hands of a man." Then, for whom were the eyes created? They were not created for themselves. Did my eyes come into existence for me or for others? For what purpose did they come into existence? They were created for the other. The nose was also created for the other. Therefore, seeing is for the other, smelling is for the other, listening is for the other, and speaking is for the other. Isn't speech created for the other? Thus, working and going should also be for the other. This is theoretical. 

When viewed this way, did women live for women? "No." Then for whom? For men, for men! You need to understand that the purpose, origin, and process of a woman's existence is for men, for men. Who is it for? "Men." Then what about men? What are men for? "Women." Women! Therefore, since both need each other, they are destined to meet. 

Under the concept of love, God exists. Then, when can all these five senses, which were created for the sake of love, develop to their fullest? When can they reach their highest point? When is it? "When they know love." That's right. It is during puberty. What if it is the opposite? This is above, and this is below. The above is man, and the below is woman. How does that feel? It feels uncomfortable, right? It goes up. It rises up. How about American women? Since women are below, it feels uncomfortable, right? (While drawing a picture) It is physiologically that way. Women are vessels. They are meant to become one through love. 

Where are babies born? They are born here. Now, you are the original bloodline, but where does the original "I" start? From the love of your parents. That's right, isn't it? "Yes." Which comes first, your life or love? What is it? "Love." Then, which comes first, God or love? "They are the same." This is a big issue. Love comes first. So how should this be interpreted? When we say that God began to exist for the sake of love, it makes sense. It means that He began to exist for love. Love is already established in the environment, and I began to exist within it. 

Love is invisible. God exists centered around love. Therefore, we must answer that God exists under the concept of love. That is how it aligns with theory. God cannot exist without the concept of love. Why? Because humans are born with love as their environment. Since they began to exist centered around love, God must also do the same. 

Now, what is the origin of this consciousness? It is the same. It all starts from love. The eyes began from love, so they live in love, they follow love, and everything is like that. They are destined to go toward the purpose of love. The same goes for the nose and all cells. When you touch, you try to touch the person you love and seek the person you love. That is not strange. It is because the original is like that, and it cannot be otherwise. 

Since it started from love, when a baby is born and cries "Wah—", the parents say, "Oh, oh." That is love. Would they say, "Why are you crying? You little brat, why are you crying? Why are you crying as soon as you come out?" (Laughter) "They wouldn't." Even if they wet themselves or poop, they feel love. Right? Do they record that in a notebook, saying, "I gave you $5, $7 each hour"? "No." They want to give and give and give again, right? So, what happens if you keep giving? If you keep giving, it all becomes receiving. 

In the dynamics of the universe, input and output work like this. (While writing on the board) If the external world's force is like this, and the internal world is like that, everything flows to one place, "Whee!" It flows away, into the universe. There cannot be a stagnant movement. "Father, are you saying that the input is large?" The input is large, while the output is small. 

Now, what is the opposing force to this? Where does this exist? This is the power of love. This is how balance is achieved. How does God exist eternally? Because of this logic, the more you act in this way, the more you can continue to exist. If you move alone, all your strength will be consumed, yet to exist eternally means that there is one principle, the principle of love. This principle of love acts in opposition. It is contrary to physical phenomena. Why is it like that? It is because balance can be achieved through it, balance. 

One does this, and the other turns like this, right? Do you understand? "Yes." This is a great discovery. The logic of eternal life is possible because of the action of love based on this principle. Therefore, it is scientific that we humans also live eternally centered around love. To be born from love, to grow in love, and to go through love means to live eternally in that place; this is theoretical. You need to understand that. Do you understand? "Yes." So, the conclusion is that eternal life is only possible through love. 

That is why the Unification Church says, "Give for the world, give! Sacrifice for the country, sacrifice! Keep giving!" But there is nothing to give? True love is something that can give eternally and still have more left over. You must be able to possess that. If someone who truly loves you gave you a hundred, when you repay them, do you want to give back more than a hundred, or do you want to give back ninety? What is your true heart? "More than a hundred." Where does that feeling come from? From love. That is how the principle of love works. 

The original bloodline breathes and lives eternally in the world of love. When you look at the original love, where does it start? From the original self, from the original parents, then through the original couple, and where does it go? It comes here and turns. This turns like this, and then when it comes here, what happens? It turns here, and then the direction changes. It comes from a different direction. 

The mother’s side and the father’s side must face each other and turn. This must turn for me to ascend. It must turn. The mother’s breath and the father’s breath must match in rhythm. In other words, you must be born in a place of joy and satisfaction. You were born in that place, where both your mother and father are happy. You were born there, grew up with siblings, then grew up with a spouse, and then learned all the principles of life. In three stages. And then, finally, you gain consciousness. Humans live forever with the idea that they are the center of the universe, with that kind of consciousness. They live in love. 

So, what kind of place is the spirit world? The spirit world is the eternal world, and all the air in that world is love; this is theoretical. Now, what should we do here? The original person is the original bloodline, and the one who has received the original bloodline must go through three stages. What is this? It is the expectation of a son-in-law. I am connected through the love of siblings, the love of parents, and the love of God. Up to the love of spouses... 

In the womb period, you live in water. There, you live in water, but what must you center on? You breathe with your belly, but in the future, you must breathe at a higher level. Your respiratory organs will change. You have a nose, but you must not breathe through it. You breathe air, but to breathe perfect air, you must block your nose. Now, if this gradually enters the respiratory system, you must destroy all of this and come out. You must cut this off, and the mother’s womb and all the water bags must be destroyed to come out. What is that? It means that your home, the womb, and the water bag, all that environment must be destroyed. It is death. The underwater world signifies destruction and the end, and a new beginning emerges. 

Then, what is the place of birth today? It is the womb of the universe. It is the womb of the universe, like a mother. What is like water? It is air, air. What do you live centered around? What do you receive from the umbilical cord? Love. You breathe love and live centered around love. You are currently training centered around love that is not perfect love. "Are you talking about here? (Interpreter)" That's right. Just like living in the womb and breathing air, we are born in this universe and are now breathing centered around love. 

Now, just like blocking the nose, only when the complete body of love emerges can you finally breathe. (Speaking while blocking the nose) That destroys this world. When you cut everything off and restart, at that time, what happens? You belong completely to the authority of love. You must understand that this is what death means. Therefore, life on this earth is all about training to create the organs that can breathe love. You must prepare a training base where cells can adapt one hundred percent to the stimulation of love. That is why here, love is air. You are being born into the world of love. 

Now, what is this? It is being born in the womb of the universe, in the divine womb. You are entering the world of divine womb. Do you understand what I mean? Divine womb. The divine nature is what we call God's character, right? We are born in the divine womb, in God. 

What does that mean? It means becoming the center of the universe in the consciousness concept. The center of the universe centered around love, the subject of all things, the owner who can govern everything. You also have the heart of being the center of the universe, right? That is what it is for. Where does that heart come from? 

So, just as God exists in the environment of love, just as God exists centered around love, I exist in love. I am within the conscious realm of God. Therefore, at that time, you must undergo the three-stage resurrection. You must understand that there is one more dimension left to enter the divine world within the realm of love. At that time, you may or may not have a body. You can do it freely, just like God. 

The sacrificial service is for completing the second respiratory organ (love). 

Since it is structured this way, we humans need love, and we have the consciousness that we will become the center. Then, where does this consciousness come from? From God. It starts here, and then it goes on, splitting into two, feeling stimulation here and moving forward. If you live on this earth and die, you enter this divine world and ascend. What is this? It is one circle, but it is one seed. Let's take a look at the seed. When you say "seed," it symbolizes the universe. (Pointing to the drawing) Every seed symbolizes the universe. They all resemble each other. That is why when you look at seeds, they are all covered with a layer on both sides. 

Now, from here, a sprout emerges. From here, a new world begins. Now, what is this? This becomes fertilizer. The mother who gave birth to you becomes the fertilizer. Isn't that right? Then, the universe becomes the fertilizer, this universe. The universe is also two. Plus (+) and minus (-). It is exactly the same. This world is also male and female, plus and minus, and is structured relatively. So, it grows like this. 

Then, what does it eventually return to? It returns as a flower that bears fruit. What is a flower? It is puberty, puberty. So, you seek a woman and seek a man, right? You say, "I love you," or "I need your love," and so on... Then what happens? It bears fruit, fruit. So, what does it mean to bear fruit? In our Unification Church, it is said that God exists as the dual characteristics; this is an amazing logic. You must understand this. Here, Adam and Eve were born. It is the same principle. So, where do we return to? After being born, we return to God Himself from the time of being a fetus. 

To interact with the universe, you must have love. If you do not have love, you cannot interact. You can never interact eternally. That is why you need love. Do you understand? When love is described as gentle and humble, it is to exercise it more and more, completely. It is a method to exercise without resistance. If you are gentle, humble, and sacrificial, you can go anywhere without resistance. You can go anywhere. Do you understand? It is for going without resistance. 

This is not sacrifice. It is a secret method to act without resistance, to live for others and serve sacrificially. Is this theoretically organized? Why must it be so? Why, why, why? Why must you sacrifice and serve? It is to complete all the respiratory organs of the second life. It is the same. If this comes out, it will grow by receiving the nutrients of the earth and sunlight. It is just like a person, this. "Like a plant? (Interpreter)" It is the same as a plant or a person. This is in three stages; it is theoretical that a person is also in three stages. Therefore, whether the spirit world exists or not is a logical contradiction. 

Who would have thought that the larvae of cicadas, which are just in the ground, would become cicadas and fly away? Shedding the shell to become a cicada is death. Do you understand? That is death, shedding the shell. People are the same. Do you understand? What the teacher is talking about here is for that to happen. You must become a friend of God in the spirit world in the future. What am I doing here on earth now? I am doing this to become a friend of God, to become like God, to become a person like God. 

Let’s become super couples with the love of the True Parents and fly through the universe. 

Now, you have a fear of death, but you must understand that death is the beginning of a new world. Do you understand? At that time, you know how difficult it is to escape the gravitational field, just like a satellite. But once you enter, when you enter the weightless world, you will just move freely and eternally. It is a world without resistance. Only then can you travel through the entire universe; when will you follow God, who governs the universe? 

Don’t you all want to visit the Diamond Star? "I want to go." How about the Gold Star? How about the Silver Star? These are all our stages of activity. The great universe. Even if it takes hundreds of millions of light-years to get there, we humans can come and go in an instant. That is the privilege of humans. Even if it took hundreds of millions of light-years, we can go to places that still cannot be reached from Earth in an instant and engage in activities. That is the greatness of humanity.
How is it? Do you all want to live here forever, or do you want to go there? "I want to go there." Here, receiving blessings from the teacher, the two of us are 'whoosh'—what is it? There’s a movie where people fly around, right? Superman. At that time, we are not Superman, but a super couple, a super husband, a super wife, flying around. (Laughter) 

Now, next, there is the plug of the True Parents here, and the fact that there is a code of True Parents means marriage. When you connect this, 'vroom,' it goes. You have to ride with the love of True Parents for the engine to run and take off. The teacher is thinking like this, so you can’t imagine how curious I am. "Wow! If I have to see the entire universe without resting for thousands of years here, how fun would that be!" This is what I think. Now, that doesn’t mean it’s far away. If you look at it this way, no matter how far it is, it appears right in front of you.

Now, when you believe in the Unification Church and go to the spirit world, will you look for the teacher or not? "I will look for him." When you take a quick look, you already know everything. When you enter, just hearing the sound, you already know everything. Those who have worked one hundred percent for the purpose will quickly return to the teacher. Those who haven’t done so, even if they call, they will rather do this. "Even if I call the Father’s name?" (Interpreter) Those who have been loyal for the purpose will turn back when they hear the call. However, those who have not acted according to the purpose will do the opposite when they hear the call. Automatically... So what can I do? Even if you don’t want to, I have the responsibility to train you to pass that world, so even if I have to make your life difficult here, I will forcefully train you.

On the day we surpass the resurrection realm of the third stage, we will become God. 

Just as you can experience this air in the womb, you must be able to breathe in the air of love. Are you prepared? You need to prepare for that. For the universe, for God. Isn’t this center God’s center? Then, on the day I resurrect and surpass the third stage, it means I become God. Creation is for making God. It is to create God centered on love. That is the image of humanity, but these foolish beings! How wretched these humans are, they are worse than insects. They are worse than insects. Is that good? You brats, is that good? "No." So, do you want to receive training or not? "I will receive it." 

Pretty girls, you know, "I look so pretty, but the partner that the teacher saved is ugly. Oh my, there are so many handsome men outside!" Isn’t that so? "No." Some women are sensitive, but to such a person, they are given a dull, what should I say? A terribly dull man. (Laughter) 

Still, you must love. That’s how you become a person. If the two can love sensitively, how wonderful would that be? That is the ideal wife, the ideal husband. Do you understand? God only created 95 percent, right? The rest is for you to create. How wonderful is that? The ideal man is created 95 percent by me. How wonderful is that? That’s how you can become the ideal man and the ideal woman. 

Right now, I am making you. You brats! (Hitting the members. Laughter) This is the ideal person and the ideal teacher. Why do you suffer without knowing how time passes? It’s because there is love in it. When you go to the East Garden, you can’t stand because your legs hurt. (Expressing with actions) (Laughter) Because you have the concept of love, you can do everything; otherwise, you can’t do anything. If you don’t like it, would you do it? 

So, you need to understand that we are meant to go through this ideal resurrection realm of the third stage. You must live accordingly. The term "blood lineage" refers to those who have a lineage. Your faces are all connected. The eyes are your grandparents. What about the nose? They are your own Buddhas. What is this (pointing to the mouth)? This is the son and daughter. This is where the sons and daughters come from. These are one organ. So, everything is connected. It all connects; it’s not separate, one by one. It must be connected. Do you understand? That’s why I exist for the Father, and I exist for the eyes. Now, I exist for this and for this. This must move completely without obstruction to be one blood lineage. (Pointing to the drawing)

Now, when the face is reborn, do you want to change the eyes? Do you all want to change your eyes? "No." These are your grandparents. Is it good for your grandparents to have married and then divorced? "No." There are two nostrils, and these are your parents. But is it good to split this and attach a different nose? "No." Also, is it good to swap siblings? "No." You want the original. The original is both the first and the process and the end. It is the inheritance to the end. The original is not something to forget. The original is something you always carry with you. 

Let’s become the original male and female and establish the original blood lineage. 

So, what kind of person is a completed person? Let’s conclude. To become a completed woman, you must be able to digest all kinds of grandmothers—good grandmothers, bad grandmothers, terrible grandmothers, all kinds of grandmothers. Even the grandmothers who spit, urinate, and defecate, and make you run errands... You must be able to face all of that joyfully, never getting annoyed, and be able to treat them as friends, always being able to treat them joyfully to become a complete woman. And not only that, but also with grandfathers. (Laughter) "Why aren’t you sleeping, why aren’t you eating, why is this happening? Why do you keep doing this?" You shouldn’t say that; you must be able to digest all of that. When the grandfather dies, you must be able to say, "Oh, I can’t forget you." 

Then what? The husband and wife. Even if the husband makes life difficult for the wife, hits her, and does all sorts of things, even if he does all the wicked things that men do in the world, you must repay it with patience and love. You must love. You must be able to subdue him with love. The same goes for the opposite. Also, the same goes for siblings. Then, the same goes for sons and daughters. This makes a total of six. You must go through one, two, three, four, five, and six to complete the seventh. The sixth is called the number of Satan, so think, "Ah! There are all kinds of Satans in our family." (Laughter) The saying that your family members are enemies will be understood when you go to heaven. 

So, when you die, you must make it so that "You are the best, you are the best, you are the best in our house," and everyone must say, "You are the best." When you die, you must make it so that you can say, "I will bless you and leave." You must make it so that you can say you will give everything. Such a person is a completed person. Is there anyone who objects to this conclusion? "No." When I say, "God, that’s wrong!" God will say, "Your words are perfect." 

Now, what kind of God is a completed God? It’s the same. When everyone dies, they must perform a spectacle that can give glory to God. Only then will everyone say, "Amen!" Therefore, not being able to live is not a bad thing. It is to grant authority. The authority of grandfathers, the authority of grandmothers, the authority of husbands, the authority of sons, it is all to give that authority. 

So, Jesus also set this standard, and saints had to go this way. Reverend Moon is now trying to walk this path. Now, because the mother is so good, she makes such a good expression. So, "Since the mother is so good, I need to experience the opposite, but there’s no such woman, so I will be trained by American women." Isn’t that wonderful? How wonderful is that? Everyone, how about it? What kind of person will you become? If you can say that your heart is the heart of the cosmic mother and the cosmic father, isn’t that God? So, when I say, "I am the great completed human," Satan must say "yes," and God must also say "yes." 

So, when you go to News World, who is the editor-in-chief? "Robert Morton." Yes, Robert Morton. What kind of person is Robert Morton? He is someone who says good is good and bad is bad. I am not like that. "I will listen to everything, and even if it’s bad, I will just think positively and digest everything, and even if it’s more difficult, I will go." This is what I think to be the person responsible for News World. Already, the coffin comes out. No matter where you go, the coffin comes out. Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." Do you understand how wonderful this conclusion is? Therefore, you must think of this process as "a stamp to pass me into heaven." 

If you receive such training, even if you meet different countries, different people, different nations, wherever you go, you will pass and have more than enough. If you try to live treating others like grandfathers and grandmothers, like mothers and fathers, like siblings, who would oppose that? Who wouldn’t welcome it? That extended world is heaven. It’s the same. Now, you have understood that by becoming the original person, going through the original lineage, you become the original completed male and female. 

Now, among the thoughts of the teacher who has this concept and the thoughts you have, which one should you have? "The Father’s thought." That is the most difficult. How can you have that concept? Everyone dislikes it. (Laughter) So, you must decide, "I will choose this." That is great. That is an amazing and wonderful thing. (Laughter) Will you try it? "Yes." (Applause)
